2010</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Dear
Shareholder and/or Friend of Zion...</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">This past
week, Israel has been in the news (again) as the 31 members of the group of rich
nations, the OECD (<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Organisation for Economic
Cooperation and Development</font>) unanimously voted to invite Israel to
join.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">OECD&#8217;s
mission is to enhance cooperation among members while meeting high international
economic standards; membership will surely boost Israel's economic standing and
help attract investment to Israel.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Israeli Finance Minister called the move "<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">historic</font>".</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We
believe that the day will arrive when Zion Oil's work will also be deemed
"historic" and are steadily working towards that day.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Here is a
report of Zion's work during the past two weeks:</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Rights
Offering</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Under the
rights offering (see <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.zionoil.com/investor-center</font>)
Zion stockholders at the close of business on May 6, 2010, were issued, at no
charge, the following:</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">ONE</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline"> subscription right
</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">for</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline"> every </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">TWO</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline"> shares of stock
owned</font>.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Each
subscription right entitles the holder to purchase one share of Zion stock at a
price of $5.00, irrespective of the market price.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
subscription rights may be exercised at any time prior to 5:00 pm EDT on <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">June 30, 2010</font>.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">This past
week, all of our record date stockholders were mailed copies of the prospectus
and other items necessary for exercising the rights.&#160;&#160;If you were a
stockholder of record on May 6, 2010, you should begin receiving these materials
very soon.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Please
note that if you hold shares in a brokerage account, you will need to contact
your broker to determine when and how you can exercise your rights as each
individual brokerage firm has their own timeline and procedures for processing
subscriptions.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As noted
in the press release, we plan to use the proceeds from the rights offering: (a)
to purchase a 51% interest in a new company (Zion Drilling, Inc. that will own a
2,000 horsepower drilling rig), (b) to drill further 'deep' exploration wells on
Zion's licenses in Israel (in continuation of Zion's oil and gas exploration
efforts) and (c) for general corporate purposes.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">The United States Geological
Survey (USGS Survey)</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The USGS
report (issued April 8, 2010) "<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic">Assessment of
Undiscovered Oil and Gas Resources of the Levant Basin Province, Eastern
Mediterranean</font>" has attracted much media attention in Israel. (You can
review the USGS Survey by clicking <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">here</font>.)</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As I
noted previously, the USGS Survey estimates a mean of 1.7 BILLION barrels of
recoverable oil and 122 TRILLION cubic feet of recoverable gas in the Levant
Basin... and that has caught everyone's eye, as the value of the undiscovered
oil and gas assessed in the USGS Survey amounts to approximately US$ 650
Billion...</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">and of
course all of Zion's exploration areas fall within the Levant
Basin...</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><IMG SRC="maanit.jpg"></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
drilling rig at Ma&#8217;anit</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">With
regard to 'Operations', we are now preparing for the next well, as you can
read.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Ma'anit-Rehoboth #2 Well
(M-R #2)</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">This well
is currently temporarily suspended for possible future use as an offset well to
the Ma'anit-Joseph #3 (M-J #3) well (see below) which is to be drilled a short
distance away.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Ma'anit-Joseph #3 Well (M-J
#3)</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Further
to our ongoing exploration work on the Ma'anit geological structure, we are
quickly moving forward with permitting and planning for the M-J #3 well
(targeted for the &#8216;deep&#8217; Permian geologic structure).&#160;&#160;(Deut.
33:13-16)</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Our new
well design is now finalized and we have begun the process of assembling the
various product and service suppliers needed to drill this new
well.&#160;&#160;To date we have issued (9) Requests for Quotations (&#8220;RFQs&#8221;) to
dozens of vendors addressing all the major components needed to drill and test a
well:&#160;&#160;tubulars, mud system, wireline services, well testing,
cementing, etc.&#160;&#160;The early indication is that most vendors will
participate in our RFQ process and seem quite eager to do business with us in
Israel.&#160;&#160;We have &#8216;cast a wide net&#8217; in soliciting price quotes and will
carefully analyze the results, when received, to ensure that we use the best
available resources offering Zion the most favorable overall value.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Permitting
for the new well continues to move at a very good pace with progress being made
on all fronts.&#160;&#160;We continue to move forward with both local and
governmental groups in assessing needs and working towards mutually agreeable
outcomes.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Barring
any unforeseen delays or complications, we remain on track to "spud" (i.e. begin
drilling) the well in the summer of 2010.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Elijah #3
Well</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Elijah #3 well was drilled to a depth of approximately 10,938 feet (3,334
meters) when the drill string became stuck within the Asher Volcanics section of
the hole. After recovering a significant portion of the stuck drill pipe,
progress in recovering the remainder of the pipe slowed and the decision was
made to temporarily suspend drilling operations pending further analysis of the
situation.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We have
decided to acquire additional field seismic data that will help us to resolve
certain questions regarding the geology of the area surrounding the Elijah #3
well. The timing for this work is scheduled to take place in mid-summer
2010.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">The Issachar-Zebulun Permit
Area</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Zion and
the Geophysical Institute of Israel (GII) have signed an agreement for GII, on
behalf of Zion, to acquire approximately 30 kilometers of seismic data in Zion's
Issachar-Zebulun Permit area. Permitting for seismic acquisition is already
underway and the timing for the field work is scheduled to coincide with the
seismic field work for the Elijah #3 project area.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">2010
Annual Meeting of Stockholders</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</font>- <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">in just one

Israel at 2:00 p.m. (local time) on Monday, <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">June 14</font>, 2010.&#160;&#160;If
you are planning to attend the meeting in person and would like to reserve a
